formant_f1_mean, energy_mean\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e97 features (canonical server-side)\u003c/strong\u003e: 40 MFCC + 40 delta-MFCC + 6 spectral + 2 energy + 2 ZCR + 4 pitch + (alpha=100/n)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eGP blending\u003c/strong\u003e: starts at n=10 (GP_MIN_SAMPLES), full takeover at n=20 They don't inform each other.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eKey insight\u003c/strong\u003e: Personal mood-glucose correlations can serve as soft Bayesian priors. If user A is consistently Tired when glucose \u0026lt;80, detecting Tired can nudge an uncertain glucose estimate downward.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eWhy it fits\u003c/strong\u003e: It's personal (not population), sidesteps \"no universal voice-glucose signal\", mood comes free from the same audio, and it's naturally gated by the tier system (Tier 4 = 50+ mood readings).\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eImplementation path\u003c/strong\u003e: \u003ccode\u003emood_glucose_prior\u003c/code\u003e in contextual_predictor.py — adjusts temporal prior based on detected mood, weighted by personal correlation strength. Uses same signal gate pattern (r\u0026gt;0.3, sufficient n).\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003ePrerequisite\u003c/strong\u003e: 2-3 users with 50+ mood-annotated readings to validate personal correlations are real and stable. Premature to build now.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003ePatent relevance\u003c/strong\u003e: Novel — no prior art on mood-as-proxy-for-glucose-state in personal voice models. Fits patent family #4 (confidence-aware).\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eKnown Data Issues\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-known-data-issues\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Known Data Issues\" href=\"#known-data-issues\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eTwo user ID systems\u003c/strong\u003e: SupabaseSync uses Supabase anonymous auth UUID, DataContribution uses \u003ccode\u003elocalStorage['onvox_anonymous_user'].id\u003c/code\u003e. Same user has two different IDs in Supabase. User mapping: 3adf8783↔f5bd2d85 (same person), a0456651↔65558912 (same person).\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eSupabase JSON columns return dict not list\u003c/strong\u003e: feature_vector, model_artifact, etc. Always handle \u003ccode\u003eisinstance(x, dict)\u003c/code\u003e before \u003ccode\u003eisinstance(x, list)\u003c/code\u003e when parsing.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eFeature vector dicts may have metadata keys\u003c/strong\u003e: \u003ccode\u003e_mel_scale\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003e_migrated_to_db\u003c/code\u003e, etc. NEVER use \u003ccode\u003erange(len(fv))\u003c/code\u003e to iterate — use \u003ccode\u003esum(1 for k in fv if k.isdigit())\u003c/code\u003e or \u003ccode\u003erange(N_FEATURES)\u003c/code\u003e. This has caused data drops in dashboard + wrong-dim features in training code (12 locations fixed Mar 19).\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eMixed mel scale in calibrations\u003c/strong\u003e: Pre-v2.6.0 calibrations used HTK mel filterbank (flagged \u003ccode\u003e_mel_scale='htk'\u003c/code\u003e). Post-v2.6.0 uses Slaney (no flag). BackgroundTrainer trains on both; tau=8 weighting handles transition. Cannot retroactively fix HTK→Slaney without re-extraction from audio.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" ONVOX Voice Glucose Analyzer - Project Memory","*Last synced: Mar 22, 2026 (evening)*","","## Key Metrics (HONEST)","- **Clean dataset**: 843 matched samples (±15 min window, v2_strict), 11 subjects","  - Note: some docs say \"827\" — that was pre-Wolf-rematch; 843 is current after `rematch_strict_v2.py`","- **Best population LOSO**: SVR MAE 12.48 (server), BayesianRidge MAE 13.53 (JS), r=-0.098","- **Signal detection gate**: r\u003e0.3 AND improvement\u003e10% AND p\u003c0.05 → **0/22 population stages pass**","- **Personal model**: 10-dim personal_10 subset, GP + Ridge, alpha=100/n, tau=8","- **What DOES work**: GP beats Ridge 7/10 subjects, personal hypo 4/6 subjects, temporal prior","- **Held-out validation** (Mar 22, `tools/validate_held_out.py`, 80/20 chronological blind):","  - a0456651 (250 cal): **GP MAE 7.92, r=0.604, p=0.001 → SIGNAL GATE PASS** (31% improvement over mean baseline). Ridge edge-10 MAE 13.05 r=0.09 FAIL. Ridge full-103 MAE 18.66 FAIL.","  - 3adf8783 (82 cal): GP MAE 27.36 r=-0.22 FAIL. Ridge edge-10 MAE 135.77 FAIL (features have inf/NaN from zero-variance columns in HTK data). No signal.","  - **First model to pass the signal gate on properly held-out data.** The signal is real for a0456651 but GP-specific (nonlinear kernel captures it, Ridge cannot).","- **Live production results** (Mar 17):","  - a0456651 (243 cal): GP MAE **7.15**, r=**0.779**, hypo AUROC **0.797** (sens 88.9%)","  - 3adf8783 (56 cal): GP MAE 30.24, r=0.143, hypo AUROC **0.682** (sens 83.3%)","- **Conclusion**: No population voice-glucose signal. Personal GP signal validated for 1/2 live users (250+ samples). Personal adaptation + temporal prior + hypo detection = the product.","","## Research Summary (see `stages_detail.md` for per-stage breakdowns)","- **Stages 1-12**: Data pipeline, Edge Impulse debunked, comprehensive audit, infrastructure","- **Stage 13**: HuBERT-PCA20, Glottal source, MAML — 0 signal","- **Stage 14**: Nonlinear features (entropy, fractal, TEO, wavelet, MGDCC) — 0/63 signal","- **Stage 15**: Contrastive learning (fusion, melspec, waveform) — 0/11 signal","- **Stage 16**: Quintile classification, asymmetric matching — 0/27 signal","- **Stage 17**: Dual-track contextual model — ships useful temporal-prior predictions","- **Stage 18**: Hypo detection — personal works (4/6 pass gate), population fails","- **Stage 19**: Physics-informed GP — **GP beats Ridge 7/10**, conformal + excursion detection","- **Stage 20**: SEED (distribution-aware intra-clip dynamics) — 0/16 signal, SVR best LOSO 12.88","- **Stage 21**: Windowed personal models (5.5s windows, 2s stride) — 3/10 improved","- **Stage 21b**: Delta voice features — deltas HURT 10/10; delta_only best for 2 subjects; CGM rate_of_change = label leakage","- **Stage 22**: System improvements from user 3adf8783 learnings — held-out validation (GP PASSES gate for a0456651), feature alignment fix (energy_mean→shimmer_approx, personal_10 subset, GP kernel reindex), device change detection, quality metadata, recording quality gate","- **Feature engineering exhausted** on 843 samples — diminishing returns, need more users/data","- **Voice feature fundamentals won't help**: 22 stages tested every fundamental voice aspect (F0, formants, MFCCs, HuBERT, glottal, spectral, entropy, fractal, TEO, wavelets, SEED). No population signal. More features = more false discovery risk on 843 samples. Bottleneck is data density per user, not feature expressiveness.","","## Production Infrastructure","- **Production API**: `https://api.onvox-ai.com` (Render, Python 3.11, Docker)","  - **Deploys from onvox-ai2** (NOT voice_glucose_analyzer) — `render.yaml` + `Dockerfile` in onvox-ai2","  - Old URL `onvox-voice-glucose.onrender.com` redirects but should NOT be used","  - Health check: `GET /health` returns `{\"status\": \"healthy\"}`","  - Background jobs: BackgroundTrainer (6h), ExperimentSweep (24h), CGMPoller (15min)","  - Known warning: `pipeline_versions` table missing in Supabase (uses `model_version_history` instead)","- **Frontend**: onvox-ai2 is source of truth (Lovable sync). `app/onvox-main/` is secondary reference.","  - onvox-ai2 has orb-based UI, 5-language i18n, GP excursion alerts","  - API base: `https://api.onvox-ai.com`","- **Launcher**: `launcher.py` — web control panel on :9000 (local dev)","- **WhatsApp Bot**: Twilio webhook at `/api/whatsapp/webhook`, US number: +19569966207 (old German: +491728619453)","  - `TWILIO_WHATSAPP_NUMBER=whatsapp:+19569966207` on Render ✅","  - Twilio routing: \"Default Messaging Service for Conversations\" → Integration → \"Send a webhook\" → our URL. Direct sender webhook didn't work.","  - Diagnostic endpoint: `GET /api/whatsapp/status` (shows from number, Twilio client status)","  - Predictions gated: no glucose values shown until personal model unlocked (≥5 calibrations). Population model has no signal.","  - WhatsApp uses AdaptiveEnsemble (separate from app's GP models). Calibration stored in `whatsapp_calibration` table.","- **Supabase**: Project `cqkkamaamlqlmecpzjxa`","  - Tables: readings, calibrations, profiles, anonymous_contributions, whatsapp_calibration, anonymous_consents, user_temporal_models, user_insights, voice_signal_status, user_model_config, model_improvement_events, cgm_connections, model_version_history","  - `calibrations` schema: **reference_glucose** (NOT glucose_value, NOT glucose_reference)","  - Storage: `STORAGE_BACKEND=supabase` + `SUPABASE_ANON_KEY` (prod), `memory` (dev)","- **Streamlit Dashboard**: `tools/streamlit_dashboard.py`","  - Pages: **Auto-Optimizer** (first, new Mar 17), Command Center, Model Performance, Users, Data Quality, Hypo Detection, Feature Explorer, Model Lab, Guide \u0026 Export","  - Auto-Optimizer: `tools/dashboard_auto_optimizer.py` — sweep all users, model comparison, per-user deploy, history","  - Groq AI summaries on multiple pages (requires `GROQ_API_KEY`)","  - **Modernized (Mar 22)**: Dark ONVOX theme (Plotly + CSS), executive summary card, held-out validation tab, device \u0026 quality tab, rich data tables","- **CGM Import**: LibreLink + Dexcom CSV in `app/onvox-main/src/services/CGMImporter.ts`","- **CI/CD**: `.github/workflows/ci.yml` — lint, test, docker build, staged deploy","- **Docker**: `Dockerfile` (Python 3.11-slim), `render.yaml` for Render.com","","## Core Architecture","- **10 features (personal_10, SDK+server)**: mfcc_0_mean, mfcc_1_mean, spectral_centroid, shimmer_approx, pitch_mean, pitch_std, f0_cv, jitter_local, hnr, voiced_ratio (indices [0,1,80,99,90,91,97,98,100,101] into 103-dim)","- **10 features (edge_10, legacy)**: f0_mean, f0_std, mfcc_0_mean, hnr, voiced_ratio, spectral_centroid, f0_slope, jitter_local, formant_f1_mean, energy_mean","- **97 features (canonical server-side)**: 40 MFCC + 40 delta-MFCC + 6 spectral + 2 energy + 2 ZCR + 4 pitch + 1 duration + 2 time-of-day","- **Adaptive ensemble**: w = 1 - exp(-n/tau), tau=8, user_mean prior, blends with personal Ridge (alpha=100/n)","- **GP blending**: starts at n=10 (GP_MIN_SAMPLES), full takeover at n=20 (GP_BLEND_END)","- **Hierarchical prior**: James-Stein shrinkage in SDK — population Ridge coefficients from `voice_signal_status` (`__population__`/`population_prior`), requires n_users\u003e=3","- **On-device**: Pure JS SDK v2.6.0, zero deps, stores raw features, re-normalizes at train time","  - Storage: `onvox_cal_v7` key; tau=8 synced everywhere","  - v2.5.0: Fixed MFCC log scale (ln → 10*log10 dB), v2.6.0: Fixed mel filterbank (HTK → Slaney + norm)","- **Validation**: Temporal chronological splits (70/30 or expanding-window for 50+ samples)","- **Contextual predictor**: temporal_prior(t) + delta_gate*voice_delta + signal_gate*voice_correction","","## ML Improvement System","- **Phase 0**: tau=8, user_mean prior","- **Phase 1**: BackgroundTrainer multi-config grid, expanding-window eval","- **Phase 1d**: SDK configurable via `/api/model-config/{userId}`","- **Phase 2**: Population regression pipeline (dormant — no signal)","- **Phase 3**: model_improvement_events + toasts in app","- **Phase 4**: `experiment_sweep.py` daily broader grid (60 configs), gate: 3+ users with 5+ cals","- **Phase 5** (Mar 9): Hierarchical prior on-device, GP at n=10, uncertainty-driven calibration nudge","- Stage labels: uncalibrated → collecting → learning → calibrating → calibrated → optimized","","## Patent Status","- **Draft filed**: `patents/CH_PATENT_APPLICATION_001_ADAPTIVE_PERSONALIZED_VOICE_GLUCOSE.md`","- **4 patent families**: (1) Adaptive personalization (FILED), (2) Residual correction, (3) EGVC, (4) Confidence-aware","- **7 prior art gaps**: no excursion detection, no gated correction, no confidence-aware voice biomarkers","- **Key design-around**: Prior art = \"glucose from voice\"; ONVOX = \"correction + gating from voice\"","- All 4 drafts in `patents/` directory + `PATENT_PORTFOLIO_STRATEGY.md`","","## App \u0026 Frontend","- **onvox-ai2 is source of truth** (Lovable sync). onvox-main is secondary/stale on many files.","- **i18n**: 5 languages (en, de, es, fr, pt) in onvox-ai2; only en, de in onvox-main","  - Key file: `src/lib/language.ts` — `getLang()`, `setLang()`, `t()`, `syncLanguageToBackend()`","  - Time-aware prompts: morning(5-11), afternoon(12-17), evening(18-4) pools in SpeechPrompt.tsx","- **onvox-ai2 UX**: Orb-based UI (CheckInOrb, ResultOrb, ModelPower, ReferenceCapture), minimal components","- **onvox-main UX** (older): RecordButton, GlucoseDisplay, CalibrationProgress, Waveform, AnalyzingAnimation","- **Sync requirements**: SDK (`onvox-sdk-103.js`) + training code (`background_trainer.py`, `experiment_sweep.py`) must match between repos","","## Data Pipeline","- **Full audit**: `docs/DATA_PIPELINE_AUDIT.md` — 22 issues, most FIXED","- Re-matched data: `data/processed/matched_data_v2_strict/` (843 samples, ±15 min)","- Feature caches: `data/processed/novel_features_cache/` (see `stages_detail.md`)","- VAD: DO NOT apply. Augmentation: DO NOT apply.","- Recoverable: ~196-349 additional samples (Wolf opus/m4a, orphaned CGMs)","- 19 total participants, 11 active, 4 audio-only, 2 CGM-only","","## Outreach \u0026 Monetization","- **User acquisition**: Facebook (FreeStyle Libre groups), Reddit (karma building, r/diabetes_t1), WhatsApp bot","  - Playbook: `docs/business/REDDIT_LAUNCH_PLAYBOOK.md`","- **Investor materials**: 15+ pitch docs in `docs/business/`, 6 in `docs/investor/`, 52 PPTX/PDF in `pitch_decks/`","  - Key docs: `HONEST_PLATFORM_PITCH.md`, `PITCH_DECK_YC_FINAL.md`, `INVESTOR_FAQ.md`, `STRATEGIC_VISION_PLATFORM.md`","- **Whitepaper**: `docs/technical/WHITEPAPER_VOICE_GLUCOSE_MONITORING.md`","- **Current strategy**: Personal adaptation product (not population prediction). Recruit CGM users for paired data. Publish honest mixed results as scientific contribution.","- **Premium/subscription**: `onvox/api/services/subscription.py`, `onvox/api/routes/subscription.py` (Stripe integration, currently disabled on Render)","","## Key Files","- Models: `adaptive_ensemble.py`, `residual_voice.py`, `physics_gp.py`, `conformal_predictor.py`, `contextual_predictor.py`, `hypo_detector.py`","- Features: `edge_extractor.py` (10-dim), `canonical_extractor.py` (97-dim), `seed_extractor.py` (93/141-dim)","- Training: `background_trainer.py` (6h), `experiment_sweep.py` (24h), `signal_activator.py`, `model_checkpointer.py`, `cgm_poller.py`","- Validation: `temporal_cv.py`, `tools/comprehensive_validation.py`","- JS SDK: `onvox-ai2/public/onvox-sdk-103.js` (primary)","- Dashboard: `tools/streamlit_dashboard.py` (main), `tools/dashboard_auto_optimizer.py`, `tools/dashboard_model_lab.py`, `tools/dashboard_explorer.py`, `tools/model_lab_engine.py`","- WhatsApp: `onvox/api/routes/whatsapp.py`","- Insights: `onvox/core/insights/pattern_insights.py`","","## Bugs Fixed","- (Mar 9) CGM import button: `navigate('/cgm-import')` → `navigate('/import')` in Calibrate.tsx","- (Mar 9) SDK copy sync requirement between onvox-main and onvox-ai2","- (Mar 12) Ops Dashboard: Render API health check URL fixed from `onvox-voice-glucose.onrender.com` to `api.onvox-ai.com`","- (Mar 12) \"0 items accepted\" toast: removed alarming warning in Calibrate.tsx + Record.tsx (0 is normal on first try)","- (Mar 12) **CRITICAL: BackgroundTrainer InMemoryStorage fix** — `_get_storage()` in background_trainer.py, experiment_sweep.py, signal_activator.py now tries `get_supabase()` first. Previously, `STORAGE_BACKEND` not set on Render → InMemoryStorage → no `.client` → entire ML pipeline was dormant (no model evaluation, no config search, no hypo detection, no hierarchical prior for ANY user). Fixed in both voice_glucose_analyzer and onvox-ai2 repos.","- (Mar 15) **Double-write calibrations fix** — contributions.py was writing to BOTH `anonymous_contributions` AND `calibrations` on API upload. SupabaseSync already writes to `calibrations` with Supabase auth user_id. API was creating duplicate rows with mismatched localStorage user_id. Removed API's `calibrations` write (lines 270-284) in both repos. Existing duplicates in Supabase need manual cleanup.","- (Mar 15) **Readings dropped from dashboard** — `fetch_supabase_data()` in research_dashboard.py skipped all `readings` rows without valid 103-dim feature vectors. On-device SDK stores 10-dim edge features → all readings silently dropped → no predictions in dashboard, no pairing with calibrations. Fixed to accept readings based on `value` (predicted glucose) regardless of feature vector dimension.","- (Mar 15) **Personal Model Lab live users** — Added source toggle (Research/Live) to dashboard_model_lab.py. Live users loaded from Supabase via `load_supabase_features()`, cached 5 min.","- (Mar 15) **Data Quality production_users** — Added `_load_production_features()` in dashboard_explorer.py so Data Explorer can show live Supabase calibration data.","- (Mar 17) **CRITICAL: dict feature_vector parsing fix** — Supabase returns feature_vector as JSON objects (`{\"0\": 1.23, ...}` → Python dict), but all 8 parsing loops in background_trainer.py + experiment_sweep.py only handled list/str → `else: continue` silently dropped every calibration. Result: trainer ran every 6h producing n_samples=0 for ALL users. GP models, hypo classifiers, personal signal detection, config search ALL dormant since deployment. Only excursion_detection worked (uses glucose only, not features). Fixed by adding `isinstance(fv, dict)` before `isinstance(fv, list)` in all 8 locations. **Pattern: Supabase JSON columns → always handle dict AND list.**","- (Mar 17) **Manual GP+hypo activation** — Manually trained and stored GP model + hypo classifier for users 3adf8783 (GP MAE 30.24, hypo AUROC 0.682) and a0456651 (GP MAE 7.15 r=0.779, hypo AUROC 0.797 sens 88.9%). Data is clean.","- (Mar 17) **CRITICAL: BackgroundTrainer blocking event loop** — dict fix unblocked ML pipeline, but synchronous sklearn model fitting blocked asyncio event loop → /health never responded → Render marked API DOWN. Fix: `asyncio.to_thread()` for all 10 `_evaluate_*` calls + 60s startup delay (trainer) + 120s (sweep). **Pattern: never run sklearn/GP sync code directly in async handlers — always use `asyncio.to_thread()`.**","- (Mar 19) **CRITICAL: SDK MFCC feature space mismatch** — Two bugs made JS SDK features fundamentally different from Python/librosa:","  1. **Log scale**: `Math.log` (ln) vs `10*log10` (dB) — factor of 4.3429x. Fixed in SDK v2.5.0 (storage v6).","  2. **Mel filterbank**: HTK formula (`2595*log10(1+hz/700)`) vs Slaney (piecewise linear/log) + no bandwidth normalization vs `norm='slaney'`. Caused MFCC correlation of **-0.82** between SDK and server. Fixed in SDK v2.6.0 (storage v7). Now correlation **0.9999**.","  - Migration: 327 Supabase calibrations migrated (log fix + `_mel_scale='htk'` flag). Old on-device samples flagged `_mel_scale='htk'`. Models will adapt via tau=8 weighting as new Slaney-scale features accumulate.","  - **Pattern**: When porting DSP algorithms to JS, verify EVERY parameter (log base, mel formula, normalization) against the reference implementation. Comments saying \"matches librosa\" don't mean it does.","- (Mar 19) **Developer API** — New `/api/v1/developer/*` endpoints (register users, calibrate, predict, model status, insights, usage). Population model has no signal, showing numbers erodes trust. Before calibration: \"Voice sample received! X/5 calibrations...\" After: actual estimate.","","## Mood-Glucose Cross-Estimation (Future — Not Yet Implemented)","- **Current state**: Mood (VoiceMood) and glucose are estimated independently from the same voice features, displayed side-by-side. They don't inform each other.","- **Key insight**: Personal mood-glucose correlations can serve as soft Bayesian priors. If user A is consistently Tired when glucose \u003c80, detecting Tired can nudge an uncertain glucose estimate downward.","- **Why it fits**: It's personal (not population), sidesteps \"no universal voice-glucose signal\", mood comes free from the same audio, and it's naturally gated by the tier system (Tier 4 = 50+ mood readings).","- **Implementation path**: `mood_glucose_prior` in contextual_predictor.py — adjusts temporal prior based on detected mood, weighted by personal correlation strength. Uses same signal gate pattern (r\u003e0.3, sufficient n).","- **Prerequisite**: 2-3 users with 50+ mood-annotated readings to validate personal correlations are real and stable. Premature to build now.","- **Patent relevance**: Novel — no prior art on mood-as-proxy-for-glucose-state in personal voice models. Fits patent family #4 (confidence-aware).","","## Known Data Issues","- **Two user ID systems**: SupabaseSync uses Supabase anonymous auth UUID, DataContribution uses `localStorage['onvox_anonymous_user'].id`. Same user has two different IDs in Supabase. User mapping: 3adf8783↔f5bd2d85 (same person), a0456651↔65558912 (same person).","- **Supabase JSON columns return dict not list**: feature_vector, model_artifact, etc. Always handle `isinstance(x, dict)` before `isinstance(x, list)` when parsing.","- **Feature vector dicts may have metadata keys**: `_mel_scale`, `_migrated_to_db`, etc. NEVER use `range(len(fv))` to iterate — use `sum(1 for k in fv if k.isdigit())` or `range(N_FEATURES)`. This has caused data drops in dashboard + wrong-dim features in training code (12 locations fixed Mar 19).","- **Mixed mel scale in calibrations**: Pre-v2.6.0 calibrations used HTK mel filterbank (flagged `_mel_scale='htk'`). Post-v2.6.0 uses Slaney (no flag). BackgroundTrainer trains on both; tau=8 weighting handles transition. Cannot retroactively fix HTK→Slaney without re-extraction from audio.","","## Next Steps (Mar 22, 2026)","1. **Run SQL migration** — `migrations/add_quality_metadata_to_calibrations.sql` in Supabase SQL editor (then re-add device_info to trainer SELECT)","2. ~~Push onvox-ai2~~ ✅ — deployed with WhatsApp fix, prediction gate, mood persistence, dashboard modernization","3. **Swiss patent filing** — now backed by **held-out validated** evidence (GP MAE 7.92, r=0.604, p=0.001)","4. **Recruit CGM users** — Facebook posts up, Reddit karma building, WhatsApp bot live ✅","5. **Populate hierarchical prior** — needs 3+ users with 10+ cals","6. **Fix remaining data pipeline issues**: partial upload data loss (DataContribution.ts:230)","7. **Fix landing page** — \"3000+\" samples claim is wrong (843 matched)","8. **Publish mixed results** — 22 stages honest negatives + personal GP positive (held-out validated) = scientifically valuable","9. **Scale to 50 users x 200 samples** — personal models need density, not breadth","10. **Mood-glucose cross-estimation** — build `mood_glucose_prior` once 2-3 users reach Tier 4 (50+ mood readings)","11. **WhatsApp → GP model integration** — connect WhatsApp bot to personal GP models from `voice_signal_status` (currently uses separate AdaptiveEnsemble). <li><strong>Clean dataset</strong>: 843 matched samples (±15 min window, v2_strict), 11 subjects
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Note: some docs say "827" — that was pre-Wolf-rematch; 843 is current after <code>rematch_strict_v2.py</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Best population LOSO</strong>: SVR MAE 12.48 (server), BayesianRidge MAE 13.53 (JS), r=-0.098</li>
<li><strong>Signal detection gate</strong>: r&gt;0.3 AND improvement&gt;10% AND p&lt;0.05 → <strong>0/22 population stages pass</strong></li>
<li><strong>Personal model</strong>: 10-dim personal_10 subset, GP + Ridge, alpha=100/n, tau=8</li>
<li><strong>What DOES work</strong>: GP beats Ridge 7/10 subjects, personal hypo 4/6 subjects, temporal prior</li>
<li><strong>Held-out validation</strong> (Mar 22, <code>tools/validate_held_out.py</code>, 80/20 chronological blind):
<ul dir="auto">
<li>a0456651 (250 cal): <strong>GP MAE 7.92, r=0.604, p=0.001 → SIGNAL GATE PASS</strong> (31% improvement over mean baseline). Ridge edge-10 MAE 13.05 r=0.09 FAIL. Ridge full-103 MAE 18.66 FAIL.</li>
<li>3adf8783 (82 cal): GP MAE 27.36 r=-0.22 FAIL. Ridge edge-10 MAE 135.77 FAIL (features have inf/NaN from zero-variance columns in HTK data). No signal.</li>
<li><strong>First model to pass the signal gate on properly held-out data.</strong> The signal is real for a0456651 but GP-specific (nonlinear kernel captures it, Ridge cannot).</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Live production results</strong> (Mar 17):
<ul dir="auto">
<li>a0456651 (243 cal): GP MAE <strong>7.15</strong>, r=<strong>0.779</strong>, hypo AUROC <strong>0.797</strong> (sens 88.9%)</li>
<li>3adf8783 (56 cal): GP MAE 30.24, r=0.143, hypo AUROC <strong>0.682</strong> (sens 83.3%)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Conclusion</strong>: No population voice-glucose signal. Personal GP signal validated for 1/2 live users (250+ samples). Personal adaptation + temporal prior + hypo detection = the product.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Research Summary (see <code>stages_detail.md</code> for per-stage breakdowns)</h2><a id="user-content-research-summary-see-stages_detailmd-for-per-stage-breakdowns" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Research Summary (see stages_detail.md for per-stage breakdowns)" href="#research-summary-see-stages_detailmd-for-per-stage-breakdowns"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Stages 1-12</strong>: Data pipeline, Edge Impulse debunked, comprehensive audit, infrastructure</li>
<li><strong>Stage 13</strong>: HuBERT-PCA20, Glottal source, MAML — 0 signal</li>
<li><strong>Stage 14</strong>: Nonlinear features (entropy, fractal, TEO, wavelet, MGDCC) — 0/63 signal</li>
<li><strong>Stage 15</strong>: Contrastive learning (fusion, melspec, waveform) — 0/11 signal</li>
<li><strong>Stage 16</strong>: Quintile classification, asymmetric matching — 0/27 signal</li>
<li><strong>Stage 17</strong>: Dual-track contextual model — ships useful temporal-prior predictions</li>
<li><strong>Stage 18</strong>: Hypo detection — personal works (4/6 pass gate), population fails</li>
<li><strong>Stage 19</strong>: Physics-informed GP — <strong>GP beats Ridge 7/10</strong>, conformal + excursion detection</li>
<li><strong>Stage 20</strong>: SEED (distribution-aware intra-clip dynamics) — 0/16 signal, SVR best LOSO 12.88</li>
<li><strong>Stage 21</strong>: Windowed personal models (5.5s windows, 2s stride) — 3/10 improved</li>
<li><strong>Stage 21b</strong>: Delta voice features — deltas HURT 10/10; delta_only best for 2 subjects; CGM rate_of_change = label leakage</li>
<li><strong>Stage 22</strong>: System improvements from user 3adf8783 learnings — held-out validation (GP PASSES gate for a0456651), feature alignment fix (energy_mean→shimmer_approx, personal_10 subset, GP kernel reindex), device change detection, quality metadata, recording quality gate</li>
<li><strong>Feature engineering exhausted</strong> on 843 samples — diminishing returns, need more users/data</li>
<li><strong>Voice feature fundamentals won't help</strong>: 22 stages tested every fundamental voice aspect (F0, formants, MFCCs, HuBERT, glottal, spectral, entropy, fractal, TEO, wavelets, SEED). No population signal. More features = more false discovery risk on 843 samples. Bottleneck is data density per user, not feature expressiveness.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Production Infrastructure</h2><a id="user-content-production-infrastructure" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Production Infrastructure" href="#production-infrastructure"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Production API</strong>: <code>https://api.onvox-ai.com</code> (Render, Python 3.11, Docker)
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Deploys from onvox-ai2</strong> (NOT voice_glucose_analyzer) — <code>render.yaml</code> + <code>Dockerfile</code> in onvox-ai2</li>
<li>Old URL <code>onvox-voice-glucose.onrender.com</code> redirects but should NOT be used</li>
<li>Health check: <code>GET /health</code> returns <code>{"status": "healthy"}</code></li>
<li>Background jobs: BackgroundTrainer (6h), ExperimentSweep (24h), CGMPoller (15min)</li>
<li>Known warning: <code>pipeline_versions</code> table missing in Supabase (uses <code>model_version_history</code> instead)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Frontend</strong>: onvox-ai2 is source of truth (Lovable sync). <code>app/onvox-main/</code> is secondary reference.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>onvox-ai2 has orb-based UI, 5-language i18n, GP excursion alerts</li>
<li>API base: <code>https://api.onvox-ai.com</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Launcher</strong>: <code>launcher.py</code> — web control panel on :9000 (local dev)</li>
<li><strong>WhatsApp Bot</strong>: Twilio webhook at <code>/api/whatsapp/webhook</code>, US number: +19569966207 (old German: +491728619453)
<ul dir="auto">

<li>Twilio routing: "Default Messaging Service for Conversations" → Integration → "Send a webhook" → our URL. Direct sender webhook didn't work.</li>
<li>Diagnostic endpoint: <code>GET /api/whatsapp/status</code> (shows from number, Twilio client status)</li>
<li>Predictions gated: no glucose values shown until personal model unlocked (≥5 calibrations). Population model has no signal.</li>
<li>WhatsApp uses AdaptiveEnsemble (separate from app's GP models). Calibration stored in <code>whatsapp_calibration</code> table.</li>
</ul>
</li>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Core Architecture</h2><a id="user-content-core-architecture" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Core Architecture" href="#core-architecture"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>10 features (personal_10, SDK+server)</strong>: mfcc_0_mean, mfcc_1_mean, spectral_centroid, shimmer_approx, pitch_mean, pitch_std, f0_cv, jitter_local, hnr, voiced_ratio (indices [0,1,80,99,90,91,97,98,100,101] into 103-dim)</li>
<li><strong>10 features (edge_10, legacy)</strong>: f0_mean, f0_std, mfcc_0_mean, hnr, voiced_ratio, spectral_centroid, f0_slope, jitter_local, formant_f1_mean, energy_mean</li>
<li><strong>97 features (canonical server-side)</strong>: 40 MFCC + 40 delta-MFCC + 6 spectral + 2 energy + 2 ZCR + 4 pitch + 1 duration + 2 time-of-day</li>
<li><strong>Adaptive ensemble</strong>: w = 1 - exp(-n/tau), tau=8, user_mean prior, blends with personal Ridge (alpha=100/n)</li>
<li><strong>GP blending</strong>: starts at n=10 (GP_MIN_SAMPLES), full takeover at n=20 (GP_BLEND_END)</li>
<li><strong>Hierarchical prior</strong>: James-Stein shrinkage in SDK — population Ridge coefficients from <code>voice_signal_status</code> (<code>__population__</code>/<code>population_prior</code>), requires n_users&gt;=3</li>
<li><strong>On-device</strong>: Pure JS SDK v2.6.0, zero deps, stores raw features, re-normalizes at train time
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Storage: <code>onvox_cal_v7</code> key; tau=8 synced everywhere</li>
<li>v2.5.0: Fixed MFCC log scale (ln → 10*log10 dB), v2.6.0: Fixed mel filterbank (HTK → Slaney + norm)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Validation</strong>: Temporal chronological splits (70/30 or expanding-window for 50+ samples)</li>
<li><strong>Contextual predictor</strong>: temporal_prior(t) + delta_gate<em>voice_delta + signal_gate</em>voice_correction</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">ML Improvement System</h2><a id="user-content-ml-improvement-system" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: ML Improvement System" href="#ml-improvement-system"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Phase 0</strong>: tau=8, user_mean prior</li>
<li><strong>Phase 1</strong>: BackgroundTrainer multi-config grid, expanding-window eval</li>
<li><strong>Phase 1d</strong>: SDK configurable via <code>/api/model-config/{userId}</code></li>
<li><strong>Phase 2</strong>: Population regression pipeline (dormant — no signal)</li>
<li><strong>Phase 3</strong>: model_improvement_events + toasts in app</li>
<li><strong>Phase 4</strong>: <code>experiment_sweep.py</code> daily broader grid (60 configs), gate: 3+ users with 5+ cals</li>
<li><strong>Phase 5</strong> (Mar 9): Hierarchical prior on-device, GP at n=10, uncertainty-driven calibration nudge</li>
<li>Stage labels: uncalibrated → collecting → learning → calibrating → calibrated → optimized</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Patent Status</h2><a id="user-content-patent-status" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Patent Status" href="#patent-status"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Draft filed</strong>: <code>patents/CH_PATENT_APPLICATION_001_ADAPTIVE_PERSONALIZED_VOICE_GLUCOSE.md</code></li>
<li><strong>4 patent families</strong>: (1) Adaptive personalization (FILED), (2) Residual correction, (3) EGVC, (4) Confidence-aware</li>
<li><strong>7 prior art gaps</strong>: no excursion detection, no gated correction, no confidence-aware voice biomarkers</li>
<li><strong>Key design-around</strong>: Prior art = "glucose from voice"; ONVOX = "correction + gating from voice"</li>
<li>All 4 drafts in <code>patents/</code> directory + <code>PATENT_PORTFOLIO_STRATEGY.md</code></li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Outreach &amp; Monetization</h2><a id="user-content-outreach--monetization" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Outreach &amp; Monetization" href="#outreach--monetization"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>User acquisition</strong>: Facebook (FreeStyle Libre groups), Reddit (karma building, r/diabetes_t1), WhatsApp bot
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Playbook: <code>docs/business/REDDIT_LAUNCH_PLAYBOOK.md</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Investor materials</strong>: 15+ pitch docs in <code>docs/business/</code>, 6 in <code>docs/investor/</code>, 52 PPTX/PDF in <code>pitch_decks/</code>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Key docs: <code>HONEST_PLATFORM_PITCH.md</code>, <code>PITCH_DECK_YC_FINAL.md</code>, <code>INVESTOR_FAQ.md</code>, <code>STRATEGIC_VISION_PLATFORM.md</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Whitepaper</strong>: <code>docs/technical/WHITEPAPER_VOICE_GLUCOSE_MONITORING.md</code></li>
<li><strong>Current strategy</strong>: Personal adaptation product (not population prediction). Recruit CGM users for paired data. Publish honest mixed results as scientific contribution.</li>
<li><strong>Premium/subscription</strong>: <code>onvox/api/services/subscription.py</code>, <code>onvox/api/routes/subscription.py</code> (Stripe integration, currently disabled on Render)</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Key Files</h2><a id="user-content-key-files" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Key Files" href="#key-files"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Bugs Fixed</h2><a id="user-content-bugs-fixed" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Bugs Fixed" href="#bugs-fixed"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>(Mar 9) CGM import button: <code>navigate('/cgm-import')</code> → <code>navigate('/import')</code> in Calibrate.tsx</li>
<li>(Mar 9) SDK copy sync requirement between onvox-main and onvox-ai2</li>
<li>(Mar 12) Ops Dashboard: Render API health check URL fixed from <code>onvox-voice-glucose.onrender.com</code> to <code>api.onvox-ai.com</code></li>
<li>(Mar 12) "0 items accepted" toast: removed alarming warning in Calibrate.tsx + Record.tsx (0 is normal on first try)</li>
<li>(Mar 12) <strong>CRITICAL: BackgroundTrainer InMemoryStorage fix</strong> — <code>_get_storage()</code> in background_trainer.py, experiment_sweep.py, signal_activator.py now tries <code>get_supabase()</code> first. Previously, <code>STORAGE_BACKEND</code> not set on Render → InMemoryStorage → no <code>.client</code> → entire ML pipeline was dormant (no model evaluation, no config search, no hypo detection, no hierarchical prior for ANY user). Fixed in both voice_glucose_analyzer and onvox-ai2 repos.</li>
<li>(Mar 15) <strong>Double-write calibrations fix</strong> — contributions.py was writing to BOTH <code>anonymous_contributions</code> AND <code>calibrations</code> on API upload. SupabaseSync already writes to <code>calibrations</code> with Supabase auth user_id. API was creating duplicate rows with mismatched localStorage user_id. Removed API's <code>calibrations</code> write (lines 270-284) in both repos. Existing duplicates in Supabase need manual cleanup.</li>
<li>(Mar 15) <strong>Readings dropped from dashboard</strong> — <code>fetch_supabase_data()</code> in research_dashboard.py skipped all <code>readings</code> rows without valid 103-dim feature vectors. On-device SDK stores 10-dim edge features → all readings silently dropped → no predictions in dashboard, no pairing with calibrations. Fixed to accept readings based on <code>value</code> (predicted glucose) regardless of feature vector dimension.</li>
<li>(Mar 15) <strong>Personal Model Lab live users</strong> — Added source toggle (Research/Live) to dashboard_model_lab.py. Live users loaded from Supabase via <code>load_supabase_features()</code>, cached 5 min.</li>
<li>(Mar 15) <strong>Data Quality production_users</strong> — Added <code>_load_production_features()</code> in dashboard_explorer.py so Data Explorer can show live Supabase calibration data.</li>
<li>(Mar 17) <strong>CRITICAL: dict feature_vector parsing fix</strong> — Supabase returns feature_vector as JSON objects (<code>{"0": 1.23, ...}</code> → Python dict), but all 8 parsing loops in background_trainer.py + experiment_sweep.py only handled list/str → <code>else: continue</code> silently dropped every calibration. Result: trainer ran every 6h producing n_samples=0 for ALL users. GP models, hypo classifiers, personal signal detection, config search ALL dormant since deployment. Only excursion_detection worked (uses glucose only, not features). Fixed by adding <code>isinstance(fv, dict)</code> before <code>isinstance(fv, list)</code> in all 8 locations. <strong>Pattern: Supabase JSON columns → always handle dict AND list.</strong></li>
<li>(Mar 17) <strong>Manual GP+hypo activation</strong> — Manually trained and stored GP model + hypo classifier for users 3adf8783 (GP MAE 30.24, hypo AUROC 0.682) and a0456651 (GP MAE 7.15 r=0.779, hypo AUROC 0.797 sens 88.9%). Both now have gp_model + hypo_detection entries in voice_signal_status.</li>
<li>(Mar 17) <strong>Auto-Optimizer dashboard</strong> — New <code>tools/dashboard_auto_optimizer.py</code> page (first in sidebar). 4 tabs: sweep all users, model comparison multi-line charts, per-user drill-down with one-click deploy, history/trends.</li>
<li>(Mar 17) <strong>Duplicate calibrations checked</strong> — No localStorage UUID duplicates found in calibrations table. f5bd2d85 and 65558912 have zero rows. Data is clean.</li>
<li>(Mar 17) <strong>CRITICAL: BackgroundTrainer blocking event loop</strong> — dict fix unblocked ML pipeline, but synchronous sklearn model fitting blocked asyncio event loop → /health never responded → Render marked API DOWN. Fix: <code>asyncio.to_thread()</code> for all 10 <code>_evaluate_*</code> calls + 60s startup delay (trainer) + 120s (sweep). <strong>Pattern: never run sklearn/GP sync code directly in async handlers — always use <code>asyncio.to_thread()</code>.</strong></li>
<li>(Mar 19) <strong>CRITICAL: SDK MFCC feature space mismatch</strong> — Two bugs made JS SDK features fundamentally different from Python/librosa:
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>Log scale</strong>: <code>Math.log</code> (ln) vs <code>10*log10</code> (dB) — factor of 4.3429x. Fixed in SDK v2.5.0 (storage v6).</li>
<li><strong>Mel filterbank</strong>: HTK formula (<code>2595*log10(1+hz/700)</code>) vs Slaney (piecewise linear/log) + no bandwidth normalization vs <code>norm='slaney'</code>. Caused MFCC correlation of <strong>-0.82</strong> between SDK and server. Fixed in SDK v2.6.0 (storage v7). Now correlation <strong>0.9999</strong>.</li>
</ol>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Migration: 327 Supabase calibrations migrated (log fix + <code>_mel_scale='htk'</code> flag). Old on-device samples flagged <code>_mel_scale='htk'</code>. Models will adapt via tau=8 weighting as new Slaney-scale features accumulate.</li>
<li><strong>Pattern</strong>: When porting DSP algorithms to JS, verify EVERY parameter (log base, mel formula, normalization) against the reference implementation. Comments saying "matches librosa" don't mean it does.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>(Mar 19) <strong>Developer API</strong> — New <code>/api/v1/developer/*</code> endpoints (register users, calibrate, predict, model status, insights, usage). SHA-256 API key auth in Supabase, user scoping via <code>dev:{developer_id}:{ext_user_id}</code>. Admin-gated sensitive routes (<code>X-Admin-Key</code>). Owner-checked user routes. Structured error format with request_id.</li>
<li>(Mar 19) <strong>Mood dashboard fix</strong> — <code>anonymous_contributions.created_at</code> doesn't exist, column is <code>received_at</code>.</li>
<li>(Mar 22) <strong>Feature alignment fix</strong> — SDK PERSONAL_FEATURE_INDICES index 86 (energy_mean, hardware-dependent) → 99 (shimmer_approx, gain-independent). Added <code>personal_10</code> subset [0,1,80,99,90,91,97,98,100,101] to BackgroundTrainer + ExperimentSweep matching SDK. Fixed GP kernel PITCH_INDICES/VOICE_INDICES to match personal_10 ordering. All configs default to personal_10 instead of edge_10.</li>
<li>(Mar 22) <strong>Device change detection</strong> — <code>_filter_device_change()</code> in BackgroundTrainer. Groups calibrations by <code>{os}_{browser}_{platform}</code> from device_info column. Drops old device samples when newest device has 15+ samples. Prevents cross-device feature contamination.</li>
<li>(Mar 22) <strong>Quality metadata in calibrations</strong> — SQL migration adds <code>device_info</code>, <code>audio_duration_s</code>, <code>recording_quality</code> JSONB columns to calibrations table. SupabaseSync.pushCalibration() writes them. BackgroundTrainer SELECT includes device_info.</li>
<li>(Mar 22) <strong>Recording quality gate</strong> — Soft gate in SDK addCalibration(): checks duration &lt;2s, voiced_ratio &lt;0.25, energy &gt;0.5 (clipping), energy &lt;0.001 (silence). Warns but still stores. Returns <code>qualityOk</code>/<code>qualityWarnings</code>. Record.tsx shows warning toast.</li>
<li>(Mar 22) <strong>Held-out validation</strong> — <code>tools/validate_held_out.py</code> script. a0456651: <strong>GP MAE 7.92 r=0.604 p=0.001 → FIRST SIGNAL GATE PASS on blind held-out data.</strong> 3adf8783: all models FAIL. Ridge fails for both users. Signal is GP-specific (nonlinear kernel).</li>
<li>(Mar 22) <strong>device_info column fix</strong> — <code>calibrations.device_info</code> doesn't exist in Supabase (migration not yet run). Removed from SELECT in background_trainer.py + experiment_sweep.py. <code>_filter_device_change()</code> gracefully handles missing data. Synced to onvox-ai2 and pushed. <strong>SQL migration still pending.</strong></li>
<li>(Mar 22) <strong>Mood data persistence fix</strong> — <code>SupabaseSync.contributeAnonymous()</code> never passed context/mood to <code>anonymous_contributions</code>. Fixed: readings pass <code>{mood: {arousal, valence, label}}</code>, calibrations pass <code>cal.context</code>. Also widened <code>DataContribution.ts</code> context type from <code>{meal?, activity?, hydration?}</code> to <code>Record&lt;string, unknown&gt;</code>. Pushed to onvox-ai2.</li>
<li>(Mar 22) <strong>Dashboard modernization</strong> — 6 improvements to <code>tools/streamlit_dashboard.py</code>: (1) ONVOX dark Plotly theme (global <code>pio.templates.default</code>), (2) dark CSS with glassmorphism cards, (3) executive summary card with KPIs, (4) held-out validation tab with scatter/residual plots, (5) device &amp; quality analytics tab, (6) richer data tables with ProgressColumn/NumberColumn formatting. Removed 25 <code>template="plotly_white"</code> across 3 files.</li>
<li>(Mar 22) <strong>WhatsApp Business setup + fix</strong> — New US number +19569966207 registered as WhatsApp Business sender via Twilio. Key learnings:
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>TWILIO_WHATSAPP_NUMBER</code> on Render updated to <code>whatsapp:+19569966207</code> ✅</li>
<li>Direct sender webhook didn't work — Twilio requires routing through <strong>Messaging Service</strong> → Integration → "Send a webhook" → <code>https://api.onvox-ai.com/api/whatsapp/webhook</code></li>
<li>Added <code>/api/whatsapp/status</code> diagnostic endpoint (shows masked from number, client status, env var presence)</li>
<li><strong>Pattern</strong>: Twilio WhatsApp Business senders route messages through Messaging Services, NOT direct webhook URLs on the sender. The "Defer to sender's webhook" option doesn't work — must select "Send a webhook" on the Messaging Service itself.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>(Mar 22) <strong>WhatsApp prediction gate</strong> — Don't show glucose values until personal model is active (≥5 calibrations). Population model has no signal, showing numbers erodes trust. Before calibration: "Voice sample received! X/5 calibrations..." After: actual estimate.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Mood-Glucose Cross-Estimation (Future — Not Yet Implemented)</h2><a id="user-content-mood-glucose-cross-estimation-future--not-yet-implemented" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Mood-Glucose Cross-Estimation (Future — Not Yet Implemented)" href="#mood-glucose-cross-estimation-future--not-yet-implemented"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Current state</strong>: Mood (VoiceMood) and glucose are estimated independently from the same voice features, displayed side-by-side. They don't inform each other.</li>
<li><strong>Key insight</strong>: Personal mood-glucose correlations can serve as soft Bayesian priors. If user A is consistently Tired when glucose &lt;80, detecting Tired can nudge an uncertain glucose estimate downward.</li>
<li><strong>Why it fits</strong>: It's personal (not population), sidesteps "no universal voice-glucose signal", mood comes free from the same audio, and it's naturally gated by the tier system (Tier 4 = 50+ mood readings).</li>
<li><strong>Implementation path</strong>: <code>mood_glucose_prior</code> in contextual_predictor.py — adjusts temporal prior based on detected mood, weighted by personal correlation strength. Uses same signal gate pattern (r&gt;0.3, sufficient n).</li>
<li><strong>Prerequisite</strong>: 2-3 users with 50+ mood-annotated readings to validate personal correlations are real and stable. Premature to build now.</li>
<li><strong>Patent relevance</strong>: Novel — no prior art on mood-as-proxy-for-glucose-state in personal voice models. Fits patent family #4 (confidence-aware).</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Known Data Issues</h2><a id="user-content-known-data-issues" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Known Data Issues" href="#known-data-issues"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Two user ID systems</strong>: SupabaseSync uses Supabase anonymous auth UUID, DataContribution uses <code>localStorage['onvox_anonymous_user'].id</code>. Same user has two different IDs in Supabase. User mapping: 3adf8783↔f5bd2d85 (same person), a0456651↔65558912 (same person).</li>
<li><strong>Supabase JSON columns return dict not list</strong>: feature_vector, model_artifact, etc. Always handle <code>isinstance(x, dict)</code> before <code>isinstance(x, list)</code> when parsing.</li>
<li><strong>Feature vector dicts may have metadata keys</strong>: <code>_mel_scale</code>, <code>_migrated_to_db</code>, etc. NEVER use <code>range(len(fv))</code> to iterate — use <code>sum(1 for k in fv if k.isdigit())</code> or <code>range(N_FEATURES)</code>. This has caused data drops in dashboard + wrong-dim features in training code (12 locations fixed Mar 19).</li>
<li><strong>Mixed mel scale in calibrations</strong>: Pre-v2.6.0 calibrations used HTK mel filterbank (flagged <code>_mel_scale='htk'</code>). Post-v2.6.0 uses Slaney (no flag). BackgroundTrainer trains on both; tau=8 weighting handles transition. Cannot retroactively fix HTK→Slaney without re-extraction from audio.</li>
</ul>
